<script type="text/javascript">
    _loader.use("jquery", function () {
        var timer = null;
        var t1;
        window.drip = new Array();
        $(".e-icon-drip").mouseenter(function () {
            var corpName = $(this).data("name"), clickUrl = $(this).data("url"),floatUrl = $(this).data("floaturl"), floatClickUrl = $(this).data("floatclickurl");
            var point = $(this).offset();
            point.left = point.left - 40;
            point.top = point.top + 25;
            if ($(".e-drip-hover").length === 0) {
                $("body").append('<div class="e-drip-hover" style="top: '+point.top +'px;left: '+point.left+'px"><div class="e-corp-name">' + corpName + '</div><div class="e-drip-img"><img src="https://so.360tres.com/t01f1c1149d50153fb7.jpg" alt=""><div>水滴信用<sup>®</sup> 旗下</div></div><div class="e-drip-text"><div class="e-text-tip"><span>企业可信百科入驻企业</span> | <a target="_blank" href="' + clickUrl + ' " e-url="'+ floatClickUrl +'>查看企业可信百科</a></div><div class="e-icon-check">工商登记信息已核验</div><div class="e-icon-check">企业已通过实名核验</div></div><div class="tips-arrow"><span class="arrow-top"></span><span class="arrow-down"></span></div></div>');

                var index = $(".e-icon-drip").index(this);
                t1 = setTimeout(function(){
                    if (!window.drip[index]){
                        var imgId_drip="e_log_drip"+(new Date).getTime();
                        var img_drip=new Image;
                        window[imgId_drip]=img_drip;
                        img_drip.onload=img_drip.onerror=function(){window[imgId_drip]=null};
                        img_drip.src= floatUrl;
                    }
                    window.drip[index] = true;
                },500)

                $(".e-drip-hover a").click(function() {
                    (new Image).src = floatClickUrl;
                });

            }
        });
        $(".e-icon-drip").mouseleave(function () {
            timer = setTimeout(function () {
                $(".e-drip-hover").remove();
                clearTimeout(t1);
            }, 300);
        });
        $(document).on("mouseenter", ".e-drip-hover", function(){
            clearTimeout(timer);
        });
        $(document).on("mouseleave", ".e-drip-hover", function(){
            clearTimeout(t1);
            $(this).remove();
        });
        $(".e-icon-drip").click(function (e) {
            var e = e || window.event;
            e.stopPropagation();
            $("#eLandpage").remove();
            $("body").append("<a href='"+$(this).data('clickurl')+"' id='eLandpage' target='_blank'></a>");
            $("#eLandpage").get(0).click();
            return false;
        });
        function imgScaling (imgWidth, imgHeight, containerWidth, containerHeight) {
            var containerRatio = containerWidth / containerHeight
            var imgRatio = imgWidth / imgHeight
            if (imgRatio > containerRatio) {
                imgWidth = containerWidth
                imgHeight = imgWidth / imgRatio
            } else {
                imgHeight = containerHeight
                imgWidth = imgHeight * imgRatio
            }
            var imgMargin = ((containerHeight - imgHeight) / 2) + 'px ' + ((containerWidth - imgWidth) / 2) + 'px'
            return {width: imgWidth, height: imgHeight, margin: imgMargin}
        }
        function drawImg (imgObj, containerWidth, containerHeight) {
            var $this = $(imgObj)
            var imgWidth = $this.width()
            var imgHeight = $this.height()
            var newImgAttr = imgScaling(imgWidth, imgHeight, containerWidth, containerHeight)
            $this.attr({'width': newImgAttr.width, 'height': newImgAttr.height})
            $this.css('margin', newImgAttr.margin)
        }
    });
</script>

<script>
    _loader.use("jquery", function () {
        $("#m-spread-left a, #so_kw-ad a, #m-spread-bottom a, #so_bd-ad a").each(function(){
            if($(this).attr("rel") == "noreferrer"){
              $(this).attr("rel","noopener noreferrer");
            }else{
              $(this).attr("rel","noopener");
            }
        });
    });
    //实地认证
    _loader.use("jquery", function () {
        window.cer = new Array();
        var t2;
        function mouseDirection(wrap, ev, fn) {
            var w = wrap.offsetWidth;
            var h = wrap.offsetHeight;
            var toTop = wrap.getBoundingClientRect().top + document.documentElement.scrollTop;
            var x = (ev.pageX - wrap.getBoundingClientRect().left - (w / 2)) * (w > h ? (h / w) : 1);
            var y = (ev.pageY - toTop - (h / 2)) * (h > w ? (w / h) : 1);
            var direction = Math.round((((Math.atan2(y, x) * 180 / Math.PI) + 180) / 90) + 3) % 4;
            if(fn) {
                fn(direction);
            }
        }
        var node = null;
        $(".certification-tag ").on("mouseenter", function(){
            if($("body>.certification").length > 0) {
                $("body>.certification").remove();
            }
            var offsetLeft = 0;
            if ($(this).text() == "") {
                offsetLeft = 120;
            } else {
                offsetLeft = 50;
            }
            $(this).next().find(".arrow").css("left", $(this).offset().left - offsetLeft + "px");
            var point = $(this).offset();
            node = $(this).next(".certification").clone();
            $("body").append(node);
            node.css("top", point.top + 25 + "px");
            node.show();

            var index = $(".certification-tag").index(this);

            t2 = setTimeout(function(){
                if (!window.cer[index]){
                    var imgId_cer="e_log_cer"+(new Date).getTime();
                    var img_cer=new Image;
                    window[imgId_cer]=img_cer;
                    img_cer.onload=img_cer.onerror=function(){window[imgId_cer]=null};
                    img_cer.src=node.attr("e-url");
                }
                window.cer[index] = true;
            },500)

            node.on("mouseleave", function(){
                clearTimeout(t2);
                node.remove();
            });
        }).on("mouseleave", function(e){
            mouseDirection(this, e, function(direct){
                if (direct != 2) {
                    clearTimeout(t2);
                    node.remove();
                }
            })
        });
    });
</script>
